< Review>
This is really a nice shopping center. The only reason I gave it 3 stars is because,  if they have disabled access to the upper shops and businesses, there is no standout signage to point you in the direction of where it is. Also, the walkways, though wide enough, are in places obstructed slightly. Due to some of the merchants taking up that space with some of their merchandise. Other than that there are a nice mix of shops and professional businesses to choose from.<//Review>

< review>
All the Simmer restaurants are legit and hella good but the claw bar is top notch! Their outdoor dinning is well set up with plenty of socially distanced tables, all the friendly staff are wearing masks and heavily cleaning after each table. The food is so flavorful and addictive, I find myself craving the spicy Simmer sauce during my work day!

I get the shrimp boil with simmer sauce with the added combo of corn, sausage & potatoes, you choose the level of spice. I always get spicy and it never disappoints, I love the burn! I've also had the lobster and crab, very tasty!! The garlic butter sauce is great also! My husband can't do spice so he gets the mild in his bag and its perfect. All the seafood boils are great quality food and all the different sauces you can get are amazing! Tip- get a side of the sauce you have in your seafood boil bag so you can dip it! The simmer sauce is especially good!

We've tried alot of their food, especially during happy hour which is daily right now. The coconut shrimp appetizer is crispy and delicious with a great dipping sauce. The garlic noodles are out of this world, get it with extra toppings (garlic & cheese), so amazing! Definitely ORDER THE SHORT RIBS! 5 stars, the best in sonoma county! Authentic flavor with great quality meat, you have to try it! Surprisingly the fish sauce crispy chicken wings are FIRE! honestly never thought these would be so amazing because fish sauce you taste, don't smell and these you can smell and taste with no problem! Lol if you know then you know, GET THE CHICKEN WINGS!

They do TO-GO food also, order everything togo and it travels well!

The staff is so friendly, attentive and quick its an overall great experience! 5 stars, I always recommended this restaurant!</review>

It was only upon getting to my car and unwrapping the to-go packaging that I realized the saw-style horror show that I had walked myself into. <time>1420881943845<//time><rating>4<//rating>< Review>
I have been a customer of RV Specialists for several years now, from minor work on my RV to major work (new engine) I've always been happy with their work. A few years ago, my Catalytic Converter went out on my RV while we were on the road heading east. We stopped at a RV repair shop in Kingman AZ and got a diagnosis. The new part was going to take three days to get to Kingman, I really didn't feel comfortable with the shop so I called my guys at RV Specialist and explained my symptoms, turns out that the part the folks in Kingman was ordering was the wrong part. I limped back to Rancho Cucamonga and had the correct part installed in two days. I saved a ton of money and a bunch of time.  I recently had an engine overhaul done on the same RV and trusted the job to RV Specialists, Rob worked closely with my insurance company ensuring that I received the best parts for the repair. Needless to say I was very happy with their service and the end product.  Anyone who owns a RV knows that repairs can be costly, what I appreciate the most about RV Specialists is their honesty, I know that the work being done is exactly what I need. On several occasions they have steered me away from unnecessary repairs by either telling me that I didn't need the work done or that it could be delayed. It's hard to find a really good RV repair shop, and although they can be a bit pricey, it is well worth it knowing that you are getting a thorough job done, and at the end of the day, when you are travelling across the country with your family, peace of mind is priceless.</Review>

I am the first to admit that I am not a "go with the flow" bride and that I need to have every detail understood and taken care of to be satisfied. In the last year of planning my wedding, Galway Downs has bent over backwards and forwards in helping me get through this process despite Covid. These are the rules of the government, not the venue. They do not cancel your wedding date because of Covid and not refund you. You have the option of rescheduling your wedding on a different day using the same deposit for up to one year. If you have booked and need to cancel for whatever reason, the reality is that the contract literally addresses "pandemics" in their policy. This is business. Expecting not to be charged for a certain amount  (that you have agreed on) while having your wedding take up a Saturday for the last X months, then to decide to reschedule based on Covid regulations you feel don't fit with the vision of your wedding and then be upset because you didn't get your down payment refunded is indicative you have very limited knowledge on how businesses must operate. You have taken up a Saturday wedding slot away form all the hundreds of other brides freaking out about finding a venue for their wedding. This has not been my experience but I feel strongly enough about how great everyone at Wedgwood is and how they're doing everything in their power to help me have my dream wedding. They respond to my micro-managed repetitive emails so quickly! They answer all my questions and send me photos because I need to know what their tea cups look like, I need to know how many people will be picking up dirty plates, and I need to know if I can get to the venue as early as I am asking in order to calm my nerves the day of the wedding. Galway Downs has given me ALL of the things I'm asking for. They want you to have a wonderful wedding!!! Just communicate and ask questions and they will hold up their end of the bargain.<//Review>

< text>
I have been a customer of ATT for almost 10 years. My husband and I have been into multiple locations for various reasons. I have always called and paid the bills, changed the services, ECT. Since my husband is military the main name on the account has always been his, but I verify everything and handle all the account issues. It's never been a problem prior to this visit. I dropped my Iphone 6 in the toilet, AH! my first ever water accident. Since my husband works out of town 3 weeks a month I knew I had to get it taken care of ASAP so I had a way to contact 911 in case of an emergency. Since I'm a mother of 4 and we are often times alone. I went into this store right when it opened, armed with my debit card for the impending cost (I didn't carry the warranty, it didn't used to cover water damage!) my phone and my 4 kids (we home school). They all went to the seating area in front of the TV and I walked in and was ignored for a few minutes, until the other customer service rep (a woman) yelled at Dorian to come and assist me (He was also watching the TV). He came over and I explained what happened, and that I needed to see if I could buy a new phone. He insisted that we check for a warranty even though I knew I didn't have one, and when he found out my name wasn't on the account he said he couldn't help me because I wasn't an authorized user. I replied, ok, how can we fix that? he said my husband had to come into the store with me. I explained that wasn't possible for another 2 weeks. I have all the information and can verify the account, but he just rolled his eyes and said "That's not gonna work". So we needed a different option. He took me to an ipad, acting extremely annoyed, and made me check if we had a warranty. Which we didn't, and it showed we didn't. So then he had me log into my account and try to add myself as an authorized user. When it came to the "verification screen" it needed a number to text to complete it. Well.. my phone is toilet logged.. so that's not going to work. I asked if I could use his number, he said no. It has to be a number that's on the account. Okay. Can I use your phone to call and wake up my husband? No. Okay fine, I replied, I want to just buy a phone outright. He looked at me, annoyed and said "Do you know how much those cost??". I said, "Obviously". At this point he is acting extremely rude, I am on the verge of tears. I reply, I just need to buy a phone so I have a way to call 911 in case of an emergency. To which he says, "I can't help you since you don't have an account with us.".

I drove to the ATT in the shopping area in Converse, still crying after the way Dorian treated us. I walked in and explained what happened. They let me call my husband and wake him up, he added me as an authorized user and the assistant manager hooked me up with a non-toilet phone. And I hope he made a great commission because he deserves it.

After this visit I strongly considered cancelling my contract with ATT, but I don't want to punish myself. So instead I am going to write this review about Dorian's poor customer service skills on every format I can find.</text>

< Review>
I was nervous at first buying tires from anywhere but Les Schwab, but Nathan and his crew have bent over backwards everytime I have brought my car in.

I even came in on two separate occasions thinking they had messed up my tire balance as I had a speed vibration. Nathan smiled and checked all my wheels and we found out the rims I had bought had a bent rim.  Completely my fault, yet I didn't pay a dime.

When I brought a replacement wheel I had bought online (wish I could have bought it from them) and brought it in to switch out again they took care of me without me having to ask.

They could have easily bent me over for two tire balances and the balance on replacing the bent rim but instead made me a customer for life.

America's tire is proof that you can get tires at a good price and not sacrifice customer service. As someone who works in customer service it made all of the positives from Nathan and his crew that much better knowing how demanding some customers can be.

Buy your tires from here if you want to be taken care of even after the sale.< /Review>
